---

## Caveats

1. **Spurious correlations**: Pairings were pre-filtered by SC title keywords; residual noise is possible.
2. **Freight data coverage**: FBX indexes cover ~27 weekly observations — extend coverage for more robust validation.
3. **Outcome window sensitivity**: Results assume a 30-day outcome window; different windows will change precision/recall.
4. **Structural blind spots**: Sudden unforeseeable events cannot appear as Polymarket signals and will always be FNs.
5. **Direction mapping**: Expected freight direction is inferred from the cross-correlation sign; weak correlations (|r| < 0.10) are excluded.
